add_namespace = idaho_rework
### News Events ###
news_event = {
	id = idaho_rework.62
	title = idaho_rework.62.t
	desc = idaho_rework.62.d
	picture = event_news_WCZ_Unites_The_Rockies
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.62.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = USA
						is_ally_with = USA
						tag = FRA
						is_ally_with = FRA
						tag = IDA
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.62.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				is_ally_with = USA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.62.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FRA
				is_ally_with = FRA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.62.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = IDA
				is_ally_with = IDA
			}
		}
	}
}

### Country Events ###
country_event = { #WCZ gains ground, Stankiewicz loses trait
	id = idaho_rework.1
	title = idaho_rework.1.t
	desc = idaho_rework.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Cornered_No_More
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = IDA
		num_of_controlled_states > 10
		IDA_jeff_stankiewicz = { is_country_leader = yes }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.1.a
		remove_country_leader_trait = cornered_fox
	}
}
country_event = { #First focus event, explains the purpose of the WCZ
	id = idaho_rework.2
	title = idaho_rework.2.t
	desc = idaho_rework.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Donald_Trump_Phone_Call
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_political_power = 15
		army_experience = 5
	}
}
country_event = { #LDS take over Utah, WCZ is alerted to this change
	id = idaho_rework.3
	title = idaho_rework.3.t
	desc = idaho_rework.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_LDS_Coup_Utah
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Set country flag to unlock decision focus
		name = idaho_rework.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = wcz_mormon_coup
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #LDS take over Utah, WCZ must decide whether to expand or defend
	id = idaho_rework.4
	title = idaho_rework.4.t
	desc = idaho_rework.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Stankiewicz_Plans
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Expansion
		name = idaho_rework.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					country_exists = USA
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_DEFENSE
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_DEFEAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = wcz_expansion
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Defensive
		name = idaho_rework.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					country_exists = USA
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_EXPANSION
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LOYALTY
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_TRUMPIST
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_REPUBLICAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_CONSTITUTION
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = wcz_defensive
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Ask Trump to decide (This is intended for the A.I., so a Trump player can control what the WCZ does)
		name = idaho_rework.4.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = idaho_rework.5
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #WCZ asks Trump for direction after Mormon coup
	id = idaho_rework.5
	title = idaho_rework.5.t
	desc = idaho_rework.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Donald_Trump_Phone_Call
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Expansion
		name = idaho_rework.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_DEFENSE
          			}
					has_game_rule = {

          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path

          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		IDA = {
			country_event = idaho_rework.12
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Defensive
		name = idaho_rework.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_EXPANSION
          			}

          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_TRUMPIST
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_REPUBLICAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path

		}
	}

country_event = { #WCZ War Plan Decision, Small Protests
	id = idaho_rework.6
	title = idaho_rework.6.t
	desc = idaho_rework.6.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { #Reduce stability by 5%
		name = idaho_rework.6.a
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

# War Plan Decisions - Again #
country_event = { #WCZ Raid (WCZ POV) - Normal Success
	id = idaho_rework.14
	title = idaho_rework.14.t
	desc = idaho_rework.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Raid
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = { #WCZ net gains 250 equipment
		name = idaho_rework.14.a
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 500
			producer = FROM
		}
		army_experience = 5
	}
}

country_event = { #WCZ intervenes in the Mormon War, demands Utah subjugate (Basically a catch-22 for Utah)
	id = idaho_rework.49
	title = idaho_rework.49.t
	desc = idaho_rework.49.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Militia_3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Utah accepts the offer
		name = idaho_rework.49.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_utah_accepts_intervention
		load_focus_tree = idaho_puppet
		IDA = { 
			add_to_faction = UTA 
		}
		IDA = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MOL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SIN
				type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LAS
				type = annex_everything
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					UTA = {
						has_war_with = HOP
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = HOP
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Utah denies the offer, WCZ declares war on them
		name = idaho_rework.49.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_utah_rejects_intervention
		IDA = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.50
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = idaho_rework.55
	title = idaho_rework.55.t
	desc = idaho_rework.55.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

		name = idaho_rework.55.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		IDA = {
		# Add Utah to the faction #
			add_to_faction = UTA
		# Transfers the states #
			transfer_state = 522
			transfer_state = 117
			transfer_state = 419
			transfer_state = 393
			transfer_state = 522
			transfer_state = 488
			transfer_state = 46 #Vegas
			transfer_state = 487 #Molossia
		# Cores the states #
			add_state_core = 522
			add_state_core = 117
			add_state_core = 419
			add_state_core = 393
			add_state_core = 522
			add_state_core = 488
			add_state_core = 46 #Vegas
			add_state_core = 487 #Molossia
		# Removes traded state cores #
			remove_state_core = 520
			remove_state_core = 517
			complete_national_focus = IDA_Allies_Down_South
		}
		UTA = {
		# Transfers the states #
			transfer_state = 520
			transfer_state = 517
		# Cores the states #
			add_state_core = 520
			add_state_core = 517
		# Removes traded state cores #
			remove_state_core = 522
			remove_state_core = 117
			remove_state_core = 419
			remove_state_core = 393
			remove_state_core = 522
			remove_state_core = 488
			remove_state_core = 46 #Vegas
			remove_state_core = 487 #Molossia
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Utah accepts the offer, but wants to keep Vegas
		name = idaho_rework.55.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		IDA = {
			country_event = idaho_rework.56
		}
	}

		}

		}
	}

			factor = 0
		}
		IDA = {

			}

						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			factor = 60

      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {

						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			else_if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {

						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = idaho_rework.128.a

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}

	id = idaho_rework.129
	title = idaho_rework.129.t
	desc = idaho_rework.129.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Utah
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.129.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Colorado Lincoln Election event, Popularity change is scaled to 4% due to only owning half of Colorado
	id = idaho_rework.133
	title = idaho_rework.133.t
	desc = idaho_rework.133.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Colorado
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Republicans
		name = idaho_rework.133.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_CONSTITUTION
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		IDA = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = republican
				popularity = 0.04
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = {
					id = idaho_rework.134
					days = 1
				}
			}
			# Nevada Election Check #
			if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 46
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				46 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.138
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 46
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 46
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.138
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Arizona Election Check #
			else_if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 495
						is_ai = no
					}
				}

					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.143
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 495
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 495
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.143
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# New Mexico Election Check #

						is_ai = no
					}

				40 = {
					owner = {

							id = idaho_rework.148
							days = 5

					}
				}
			}

					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 40
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 40
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.148
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Washington Election Check #
			else_if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 125
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				125 = {

				}

						owns_state = 2
						is_ai = no
					}
				}

							days = 5

							id = idaho_rework.173
							days = 5

					}

				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.173
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			else_if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

						days = 3
					}

						days = 3
					}

					}

						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}

			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 495
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 495
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}

							days = 5

					}

						id = idaho_rework.173
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			else_if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right

					}
				}

						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}

				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}

country_event = { #Washington Lincoln Election event, Popularity change is scaled to 9%
	id = idaho_rework.153
	title = idaho_rework.153.t
	desc = idaho_rework.153.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Washington
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Republicans
		name = idaho_rework.153.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}

              			rule = IDA_path

			}
		}

					is_ally_with = ROOT

				}
			}

							owns_state = 496
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}

					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_TRUMPIST
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_REPUBLICAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		IDA = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = autocratic
				popularity = 0.09
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = {
					id = idaho_rework.157
					days = 1
				}
			}
			# Oregon Election Check #
			if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 496
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				496 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.158
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 496
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 496
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.158
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# California Election Check #
			else_if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 304
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				304 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.163
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 304
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 304
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {

						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Alaska Election Check #
			else_if = { #Player Controlled Ally

						owns_state = 2
						is_ai = no
					}

				limit = {

						owns_state = 433
						is_ai = no
					}

				433 = {
					owner = {

							id = idaho_rework.173
							days = 5

					}

					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.173
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			else_if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory

						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}

					}
				}

              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_REPUBLICAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		IDA = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = autocratic
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = {
					id = idaho_rework.167
					days = 1
				}
			}
			# Alaska Election Check #
			if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 2
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				2 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.168
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 2
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 2
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.168
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Hawaii Election Check #
			else_if = { #Player Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					any_allied_country = {
						owns_state = 433
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				433 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = idaho_rework.173
							days = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Direct Control/A.I. Controlled Ally
				limit = {
					OR = {
						IDA = {
							owns_state = 433
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							owns_state = 433
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.173
						days = 5
					}
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			else_if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Alaska Lincoln Election event, Popularity change is scaled to 3%
	id = idaho_rework.168
	title = idaho_rework.168.t

	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Alaska
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Republicans
		name = idaho_rework.168.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN

      			}
   			}
		}

				ideology = republican
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}

					days = 1
				}
			}

country_event = { #Hawaii Lincoln Election event, Popularity change is scaled to 4%
	id = idaho_rework.173
	title = idaho_rework.173.t
	desc = idaho_rework.173.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Hawaii
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Republicans
		name = idaho_rework.173.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_DEMOCRAT
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_LIBERTARIAN
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_LIN_CONSTITUTION
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		IDA = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = republican
				popularity = 0.04
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = {
					id = idaho_rework.174
					days = 1
				}
			}
			# Election Winner Events #
			if = { #Republican Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						republican > party_popularity@democrat
						republican > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						republican > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.178
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Democrat Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						democrat > party_popularity@republican
						democrat > party_popularity@libertarian_right
						democrat > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.182
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Libertarian Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@republican
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@democrat
						libertarian_right > party_popularity@autocratic
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.184
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Constitution Victory
				limit = {
					IDA = {
						autocratic > party_popularity@republican
						autocratic > party_popularity@democrat
						autocratic > party_popularity@libertarian_right
					}
				}
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.186
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Deadlock (Basically a fail safe where Lincoln can just choose who wins)
				IDA = {
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = IDA
					}
					country_event = {
						id = idaho_rework.188
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Democrats
		name = idaho_rework.173.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0

country_event = { #Trump decides whether it wants to accept Lincoln back into its faction or not
	id = idaho_rework.189
	title = idaho_rework.189.t
	desc = idaho_rework.189.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Lincoln_Declaration
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Accept the offer, WCZ and its allies will join Trump's faction
		name = idaho_rework.189.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = IDA
			}
			USA = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = IDA
				modifier = faction_traitor
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Reject the offer, USA will gain a war goal on Lincoln, Lincoln gets event to switch their branch
		name = idaho_rework.189.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = IDA
		}
		IDA = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.190
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = idaho_rework.200.a

			CAS = {
				has_government = republican
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CAS_jospeh_rice = {
				promote_character = {
					ideology = libertarian_ideology
				}
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = libertarian_right
			size = 0.5
			keep_political_leader = no
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CAS
				has_government = libertarian_right
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = IDA_Cascadia
			load_focus_tree = idaho_puppet
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Starts civil war in Cascadia (Option is if Cascadia does not have a Republican government)
		name = idaho_rework.200.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				CAS = {

				}
			}
		}

			factor = 10
		}

				promote_character = {
					ideology = trumpist
				}
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {

			size = 0.5
			keep_political_leader = no
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CAS
				has_government = republican
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = IDA_Cascadia
			load_focus_tree = idaho_puppet

	title = idaho_rework.215.t
	desc = idaho_rework.215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Militia_6
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Starts civil war in Alaska (Option is if Alaska has a Republican government)
		name = idaho_rework.215.a
		trigger = {
			ALA = {
				has_government = republican
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ALA_john_root_III = {
				promote_character = {
					ideology = libertarian_ideology
				}
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = libertarian_right
			size = 0.5
			keep_political_leader = no
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ALA
				has_government = libertarian_right
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = IDA_Alaska
			load_focus_tree = idaho_puppet
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Starts civil war in Alaska (Option is if Alaska does not have a Republican government)
		name = idaho_rework.215.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				ALA = {
					has_government = republican
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ALA_john_root_III = {
				promote_character = {
					ideology = trumpist
				}
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = republican
			size = 0.5
			keep_political_leader = no
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ALA
				has_government = republican
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = IDA_Alaska
			load_focus_tree = idaho_puppet
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Montana militias join the WCZ
	id = idaho_rework.220
	title = idaho_rework.220.t
	desc = idaho_rework.220.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Militias_1
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = IDA
		OR = {
			has_government = republican
			has_government = libertarian_right
		}
		OR = {
			controls_state = 35
			controls_state = 39
			controls_state = 64
			controls_state = 67
			controls_state = 70
			controls_state = 86
			controls_state = 118
			controls_state = 119
			controls_state = 453
			controls_state = 567
			controls_state = 570
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = idaho_rework.220.a
		show_unit_leaders_tooltip = IDA_ryan_payne
		add_manpower = 300
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 350
			producer = MON
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = wcz_montana_militias_recruited
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #WCZ chooses whether it wants National Guard advisors or Trump advisors
	id = idaho_rework.222
	title = idaho_rework.222.t
	desc = idaho_rework.222.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_National_Guard
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Trump advisors: gain republican popularity, gain army experience, gain doctrine bonus, reduce army debuffs
		name = idaho_rework.222.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = republican
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		army_experience = 50
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = land_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.75
			uses = 2
			category = land_doctrine
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = IDA_Militia_State_4 
			add_idea = IDA_Militia_State_5
		}
	}
	
	option = { #National Guard advisors: loose political power, gain autocratic popularity, gain generals and advisors, gain army experience, gain doctrine bonus, reduce army debuffs
		name = idaho_rework.222.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
      			factor = 0 
      			OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY_MODERATE
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY_EXTREME
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY_GUARD
          			}
					has_game_rule = {
              			rule = IDA_path
             			option = IDA_PATH_RMLF_VICTORY_CIRCLE
          			}
      			}
   			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_air_and_army_generals_reinstated
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = autocratic
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		army_experience = 25
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = land_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = land_doctrine
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = IDA_Militia_State_4 
			add_idea = IDA_Militia_State_5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = wcz_military_allowed_to_operate
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = autocratic 
				long_name = "Western Command - National Guard"
				name = "WC-N"
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = idaho_rework.224

	desc = idaho_rework.224.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Focus on strategic bombing, gains bonus for strategic bombing doctrine

			factor = 10
		}

		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = { 
			name = air_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.50
			uses = 2
			category = strategic_destruction_tree
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_Eagles_Of_The_West_Strategic_Destruction_Spirit
	}
	option = { #Focus on close air support, gains bonus for battlefield support doctrine
		name = idaho_rework.224.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_air_doctrine_choice
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = { 
			name = air_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.50
			uses = 2
			category = battlefield_support_tree
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_Eagles_Of_The_West_Battlefield_Support_Spirit
	}
	option = { #Focus on both (tactical bombers), gains bonus for operation integrity doctrine
		name = idaho_rework.224.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_air_doctrine_choice
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = { 
			name = air_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.50
			uses = 2
			category = operational_integrity_tree
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_Eagles_Of_The_West_Operational_Integrity_Spirit
	}
}
country_event = { #USA splits Idaho and Wyoming between the WCZ and Montana
	id = idaho_rework.225
	title = idaho_rework.225.t
	desc = idaho_rework.225.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Generic_Meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #WCZ gets this event, actually transfers the territory
		name = idaho_rework.225.a
		trigger = {
			tag = IDA
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = IDA 
				CONTROLLER = {
					tag = MON
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 99
					state = 66
					state = 63
					state = 569
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = MON
			IDA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = IDA 
				CONTROLLER = {
					tag = MON
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = IDA
		}
		IDA = {
			complete_national_focus = IDA_Request_The_Return_Of_Our_Territories
		}
	}
	option = { #Montana gets this event, doesn't actually do anything
		name = idaho_rework.225.b
		trigger = {
			tag = MON
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Passive WCZ decides what to do with friendly Montana
	id = idaho_rework.226
	title = idaho_rework.226.t
	desc = idaho_rework.226.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Montana
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Ask Montana to annex the WCZ, A.I. will do this 100% of the time
		name = idaho_rework.226.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_end_of_our_nation
		MON = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.227
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Ask Montana to annex itself into the WCZ. A.I. will never do this
		name = idaho_rework.226.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		MON = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.230
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #WCZ will ask for Wyoming and Idaho back
		name = idaho_rework.226.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = { #Do nothing
		name = idaho_rework.226.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		complete_national_focus = IDA_Open_Negotiations_With_Montana
	}
}
country_event = { #WCZ asks Montana to annex them
	id = idaho_rework.227
	title = idaho_rework.227.t
	desc = idaho_rework.227.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Montana
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Montana agrees to annex them, transfer troops and gains cores
		name = idaho_rework.227.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = IDA
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = IDA
			}
			add_core_of = MON
		}
		IDA = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_nationality = MON
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Montana rejects the offer
		name = idaho_rework.227.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		IDA = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.228
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #WCZ asks Montana to return Idaho and Wyoming
	id = idaho_rework.230
	title = idaho_rework.230.t
	desc = idaho_rework.230.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IDA_Montana
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Montana agrees to return all of Idaho and Wyoming
		name = idaho_rework.230.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = IDA 
				CONTROLLER = {
					tag = MON
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = MON
			IDA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			IDA = {
				complete_national_focus = IDA_Open_Negotiations_With_Montana
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Montana offers to split the territory 
		name = idaho_rework.230.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		IDA = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.231
				days = 3
			}
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_air_and_army_generals_reinstated
		# Add Resources #

			amount = 1000
			producer = USA
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

			producer = USA
		}

			type = motorized_equipment
			amount = 300
			producer = USA
		}
		
		# Political Changes #
		IDA_donald_trump_jr = {
			promote_character = {
				ideology = trumpist
			}
		}
		USA = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = politically_connected
					}
				}
            	set_nationality = IDA
        	}
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_The_Duumvirate
		add_ideas = IDA_Eagles_Of_The_West_Spirit

		if = {

				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = IDA_We_March_Forward
				}
			}
			complete_national_focus = IDA_We_March_Forward
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = IDA_Dig_In
			}
			complete_national_focus = IDA_Defeat_In_The_East
		}
		
		# Fixes Militia State National Spirit #
		remove_ideas = {
			IDA_Militia_State_1
			IDA_Militia_State_2
			IDA_Militia_State_3
			IDA_Militia_State_4
			IDA_Militia_State_5
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_Army_Of_The_Redoubt_2
		
		# Dependent Industry Fix #
		remove_ideas = {
			IDA_Economic_Dependence_1
			IDA_Economic_Dependence_2
			IDA_Economic_Dependence_3
			IDA_Economic_Dependence_4
		}
		add_ideas = IDA_Economic_Miracle
		
		# Create 5 Divisions #
		create_unit = {
			division = "name = \"Trumpist Exiles\" division_template = \"Veteran Combat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 0.3" 
			owner = IDA
		}

			owner = IDA
		}
		create_unit = {

                    }
				}

				}
            }

					tag = MON

			}

			}

					OR = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PRA
					autonomous_state = autonomy_colony
					freedom_level = 0.1
				}
				else = {
					puppet = PRA
				}
			}
		}
		IDA = {
			complete_national_focus = IDA_Meet_With_Jenner
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Jenner rejects the demands
		name = idaho_rework.268.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wcz_angered
		IDA = {
			country_event = {
				id = idaho_rework.269
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}
